SELECT r.role_request_id, r.created_at, r.current_role_id, r.employee_id, r.remarks, r.request_status_id, r.requested_role_id, r.reviewed_at, r.reviewed_by, e.employee_id, e.created_at, e.department_id, e.email, e.employee_name, e.is_active, e.mobile_number, e.password_hash, e.role_id, e.updated_at, r0.role_id, r0.created_at, r0.role_name, r1.role_id, r1.created_at, r1.role_name, r2.request_status_id, r2.status_name, e0.employee_id, e0.created_at, e0.department_id, e0.email, e0.employee_name, e0.is_active, e0.mobile_number, e0.password_hash, e0.role_id, e0.updated_at
FROM role_requests AS r
INNER JOIN employees AS e ON r.employee_id = e.employee_id
INNER JOIN roles AS r0 ON r.current_role_id = r0.role_id
INNER JOIN roles AS r1 ON r.requested_role_id = r1.role_id
INNER JOIN request_statuses AS r2 ON r.request_status_id = r2.request_status_id
LEFT JOIN employees AS e0 ON r.reviewed_by = e0.employee_id
WHERE r.employee_id = @employeeId
ORDER BY r.created_at DESC

FROM complaint_assignment_history AS c
LEFT JOIN employees AS e ON c.old_handler_employee_id = e.employee_id
INNER JOIN employees AS e0 ON c.new_handler_employee_id = e0.employee_id
